<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"><a href="http://www.ouyi.mymailer.com.tw/ouyihtm/Tanxu/1/06/003-6.htm#發心度生"><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">发心度生</span></span></a>   <o:p></o:p> </span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"><a href="http://www.ouyi.mymailer.com.tw/ouyihtm/Tanxu/1/06/003-6.htm#四種律儀"><span class="GramE"><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">四种律仪</span></span></span></a>   <o:p></o:p> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"><a href="http://www.ouyi.mymailer.com.tw/ouyihtm/Tanxu/1/06/003-6.htm#一斷婬"><span class="GramE"><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">一</span></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">断<span class="GramE"><span lang="EN-US"> </span></span></span></span></a>   <o:p></o:p> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"><a href="http://www.ouyi.mymailer.com.tw/ouyihtm/Tanxu/1/06/003-6.htm#二斷殺"><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">二<span class="GramE"><span lang="EN-US">断杀</span></span></span></span></a>   <o:p></o:p> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"><a href="http://www.ouyi.mymailer.com.tw/ouyihtm/Tanxu/1/06/003-6.htm#三斷盜"><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">三<span class="GramE"><span lang="EN-US">断盗</span></span></span></span></a>   <o:p></o:p> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="center"><span lang="EN-US" style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"><a href="http://www.ouyi.mymailer.com.tw/ouyihtm/Tanxu/1/06/003-6.htm#四斷妄"><span lang="EN-US"><span lang="EN-US">四断<span class="GramE"><span lang="EN-US">妄</span></span></span></span></a>   <o:p></o:p> </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><a name="六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></a></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">大佛<span class="GramE">顶首楞严</span>经卷十<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="right"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">唐中天竺</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">沙门般<span class="GramE">剌</span>密<span class="GramE">谛</span>译<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="LAYOUT-GRID-MODE: char; TEXT-ALIGN: right" align="right"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">唐清河<span class="GramE">房融笔</span>受<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="觀音耳根"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">观音耳根<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">尔时</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">。观世音菩萨。即<span class="GramE">从座起</span>。顶礼佛足。<span class="GramE">而白佛言</span>。<span class="GramE">世</span>尊。忆念我昔无数<span class="GramE">恒河沙劫</span>。于时有佛。出现于<span class="GramE">世</span>。名观世音。我<span class="GramE">于彼佛</span>。发菩提心。<span class="GramE">彼</span>佛教我。<span class="GramE">从闻思修</span>。入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">此一节文是</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">第二十五圆通，这是最后，到了结构的地方，所以必要多说，佛<span class="GramE">说这部经</span>，注意还是在耳根圆通上，第二十五是耳根圆通，是因我们<span class="GramE">娑</span>婆世界的人耳根灵，所以由耳根上修圆通接近，是这么<span class="GramE">个</span>道理，要不怎么把耳根搁在最后，这是多多的发挥发挥，让人明白，人人都会修行，「<span class="GramE">尔时</span>」，就在大势至<span class="GramE">菩萨说完</span>，随跟著他<span class="GramE">接续著</span>说，「观世音菩萨」，菩萨两个字，<span class="GramE">说具足</span>了就叫菩提<span class="GramE">萨 </span>，翻中国话<span class="GramE">就叫觉有情</span>，他自己觉悟了，再觉悟一切没开悟的有情众生，简略言之就叫菩萨，这位菩萨的别名叫观世音，<span class="GramE">他是寻声</span>救苦，听见那里有苦难的事情，你一念观世音菩萨，当时就得救，这种事情我就经过不少，实实在在是灵验，他观世间上的音声，寻声救苦，原题的本名字<span class="GramE">叫观自在</span>，就是观世音菩萨，「即<span class="GramE">从座起</span>」，各有本位，他从座位上站起来，「顶礼佛足」，对著佛顶礼，这是最恭敬的礼，「<span class="GramE">而白佛言</span>」，对佛表白说，「<span class="GramE">世</span>尊，忆念我昔无数<span class="GramE">恒河沙劫</span>」，我回想在往昔无数的<span class="GramE">恒河沙劫</span>，时间太长了，「于时有佛，出现于<span class="GramE">世</span>」，就在那个时候，有一位佛出现于<span class="GramE">世</span>，「名观世音」，名叫观世音佛，这位菩萨是后来才用的名字，叫观世音菩萨，佛法不讲犯圣讳，佛还愿意因你这个名字，把我这个名字提起来了，是这么个道理；这时候我们一个地方一个风俗，怕犯圣<span class="GramE">讳</span>，在那很<span class="GramE">久劫以前</span>，「我<span class="GramE">于彼佛</span>」，我于观音佛前，「发菩提心」，怎么叫菩提心？我自己觉悟了，「发菩提心」，再觉悟世间上一切有情的众生，我让他转<span class="GramE">情归理</span>，是叫一切众生觉悟，认识自己，「彼佛教我，<span class="GramE">从闻思修</span>，入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>」，彼观世音佛教我<span class="GramE">从闻思修入三摩地</span>，这是一入手修行，<span class="GramE">从闻性</span>发起思惟的观念，闻、思这两<span class="GramE">个字搁</span>在一块，就叫修行。人在世界上，都观念声色，<span class="GramE">都著</span>在形相上，色、声、香、味、触、法，这是六尘，都迷在六<span class="GramE">尘上</span>，不认识自己了，自己就是见、闻、觉、知；教你见自见、知自知，人自己不承认，就认识眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意是我，岂不知见、闻、觉、知才是我。由闻、思、修，闻著这种道理，转过来观念，闻自己这个闻，就是这么一句话，这个闻是常常的不断思<span class="GramE">惟</span>，这个思惟就是观念，时时不忘我<span class="GramE">这个闻性</span>，<span class="GramE">回生换熟</span>，把见、闻、觉、<span class="GramE">知都放弃</span>了，<span class="GramE">都著</span>在眼、耳、鼻、舌、身、意上，这是我们人错的地方、吃亏的地方。佛出世没有旁的，就是教人转过来自己认识自己，因为人都习惯了，<span class="GramE">拿眼</span>、耳、鼻、舌、身、<span class="GramE">意当自己</span>的，怎么办呢？你得转过这个观念来，你时时观念见自见、闻自闻、觉自觉、知自知就对了。<span class="GramE">从闻思</span>上，就是<span class="GramE">从闻性</span>上，<span class="GramE">不是从闻听见</span>我说什么话，不是这个，什么话都不用管，他说话我就闻见了，就照著我这个闻说，不讲他说的话有什么动机，就从这个闻上，你要知道这个闻是他自己，你得常常的思<span class="GramE">惟</span>，别忘了，我们这个人时时这个我忘不了，拿著我的就当<span class="GramE">了我啦</span>，这个身体是我的身体，是我使唤的物，拿这个当了自己了，自己不认得自己，这个地方才说「<span class="GramE">从闻思修</span>」，<span class="GramE">从闻常常</span>的思惟、观念，以闻为闻，也可以说观念自己这个<span class="GramE">闻性，从闻</span>这里思惟不断，以这个就叫修行，「<span class="GramE">从闻思修</span>」，修得有效验，「入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>」，先得正定正受，观念自己的闻性，不打妄想，就有正当的享受，正定、正受这叫三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">初于闻中</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">。入流亡所。所<span class="GramE">入既寂</span>。动静二相。了然不生。</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #3366ff; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「<span class="GramE">初于闻中</span>」，起初我在闻性之中，得著效验，什么效验呢？「入流亡所」，入了闻性之流，闻性是无生死的，「入流亡所」，怎么<span class="GramE">叫亡所呢</span>？<span class="GramE">亡其所</span>知，佛法不让人起执著性，我们人所执著的都是有生死的，无生死的地方就不知道了，所以这个时候就「入流亡所」，入什么流？入闻性的流，有什么好处？<span class="GramE">就亡其</span>所，他没有所执著的地方，不执著这个身体是我，「所<span class="GramE">入既寂</span>」，这个所入既然已经寂静无声，当然是有动静才显出声音，动静这二相不生出动静的这个分别相来，<span class="GramE">就观这个</span>未有的闻；<span class="GramE">闻分三样</span>，有所闻、能闻、<span class="GramE">本闻</span>，这个声音是所闻的，<span class="GramE">AN&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">如是渐增。闻<span class="GramE">所闻尽</span>。<span class="GramE">尽闻不住</span>。觉<span class="GramE">所觉空</span>。<span class="GramE">空觉极圆</span>。<span class="GramE">空所空灭</span>。<span class="GramE">生灭既灭</span>。<span class="GramE">寂灭现</span>前。忽然超越<span class="GramE">世</span>出世间。十方圆明。获二殊胜。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这段文是观世音菩萨诉说自己圆满修行的道理，他又叙说他起初修行的时候，他是跟著观世音佛学法，<span class="GramE">依闻</span>、思、<span class="GramE">修证三摩地</span>，依闻性修行也<span class="GramE">最合此方</span>人的机缘，所以观世音诉说他修行入手的法门。观世音佛<span class="GramE">指教从闻上</span>修行，自己保住了自己，<span class="GramE">不</span>随著声音转，我们普通人耳朵的闻性都随著声音转了，把声音撂下，保住自己的闻性，在闻性上起思<span class="GramE">惟</span>，不断的思惟这个闻性，要这么样修行就容易入手，最简单、也最容易明白，「<span class="GramE">初于闻中</span>」，起初在闻性之中，「入流亡所」，入于闻性之流，普通的人都随著声音转了，起初的我就入于闻性的这一流，<span class="GramE">就亡去</span>声音所污染的了，我们人不考虑自己的闻性，<span class="GramE">都著</span>在声音上了，「所<span class="GramE">入既寂</span>，动静二相，了然不生」，所入寂然不动，这个动静二相，由这里心里明明了了的，<span class="GramE">不</span>随著声音转了，「如是渐增」，如是由浅入深，渐增至「闻<span class="GramE">所闻尽</span>」，这功夫得渐渐增长，就照著这个「动静二相，了然不生」，这地方正是<span class="GramE">圆破色阴，超劫浊</span>，这是什么意思呢？这个世界是五浊的世界，五样浑浊，这五样是什么呢？色、受、想、行、识，色是有形有色的身体，有身体就得享受衣、食、住，享受就得发生思想，有思想就得有行为，行什么事就有什么认识，普通人都是这么样，世界就从这五<span class="GramE">蕴</span>上起的，人受苦也在五<span class="GramE">蕴</span>上，人人都如此，这个世界就浑浊了，你要享受、我也要享受，你想舒服、我也想舒服，这就造成五浊的恶<span class="GramE">世</span>。自古以来世界<span class="GramE">的现相都</span>摆在这里，色<span class="GramE">蕴</span>愈重，这个<span class="GramE">时劫就</span>浑浊了，把色<span class="GramE">蕴</span>破了才能<span class="GramE">超出劫浊</span>，由这里「所<span class="GramE">入既寂</span>，动静二相，了然不生」，这是说破完了<span class="GramE">色阴，这个阴也</span>有翻<span class="GramE">蕴</span>，就是积蓄的，日积月累，五<span class="GramE">蕴</span>是<span class="GramE">鸠摩罗什翻</span>的，五阴也是在唐朝翻的，<span class="GramE">所以存古还是</span>五<span class="GramE">蕴</span>，色<span class="GramE">蕴</span>就是明白<span class="GramE">这个圆理了</span>，明白<span class="GramE">这个圆理破除</span>这个色<span class="GramE">蕴</span>，就能<span class="GramE">超出劫浊</span>，就不受色<span class="GramE">蕴</span>的苦缚，说「如是渐增，闻<span class="GramE">所闻尽</span>」，这是承<span class="GramE">上边说的</span>，就这么样的修行，渐渐增长这个功夫，「闻所闻尽」，能闻的闻、所闻的这个相都尽了，能闻、所闻都没有了，这个功夫用的深入了，这一段文是圆破受蕴，超出见浊，「尽闻不住」，能闻、所闻都销灭了，我不住果，再往前进步，「觉所觉空」，能觉和所觉都空了，这都是一步步的功夫，大家要注意，就会修行，能觉、所觉都没有了，功夫用到这里，「空觉极圆」，连空带觉一切都圆满了，这是破想蕴，超烦恼浊，「空所空灭」，能空的法、所空的法都灭了，「生灭既灭，寂灭现前」，生也灭了、灭相也已经灭了，这是对待的生灭，底下是正受的生灭，「寂灭现前」，功夫到了这里，万法皆空，得大自在，寂灭是寂而不动，现前是成就大用，这是圆破行蕴，超众生浊。底下是<span class="GramE">圆破识阴，</span>以圆满的功夫破除<span class="GramE">识阴，阴是遮藏</span>之义，<span class="GramE">把识阴破</span>了，<span class="GramE">超命浊</span>，人的生命是有限的，<span class="GramE">活多大</span>岁数，到时候命就没有了，这是<span class="GramE">叫命浊</span>，把<span class="GramE">这个浊也</span>超出去了，「忽然超越<span class="GramE">世</span>出世间」，在这时候忽然之间把世间法与出世间法都超出去了，世间法是凡夫、出世间法是二乘圣人，这是大乘佛法，到这个时候「十方圆明」，十方世界都是圆满光明，功夫用到这儿得大自在，「获二殊胜」，得著<span class="GramE">两种殊</span>胜的好处，是什么呢？<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">一</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">者。上合十<span class="GramE">方诸佛本妙</span>觉心。与佛如来<span class="GramE">同一慈力</span>。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这是观世音菩萨说，「<span class="GramE">一</span>者，上<span class="GramE">合十方诸佛</span>」，头一样，往上说契合十方诸佛，「<span class="GramE">本妙觉</span>心」，人人都有本有的妙，<span class="GramE">佛证果</span>，证得不可思议的安乐，「<span class="GramE">本妙觉</span>心」根本上就是不思议的一个知觉的心，我修习这个，他对释迦佛说，「与佛如来<span class="GramE">同一慈力</span>」，都同是一样大慈悲的力量。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">二者。下合十方一切六道众生。与诸众生。<span class="GramE">同一悲仰。</span><span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这是观世音菩萨所证的果位，「二者，下合十方一切六道众生」，这六道有天道，也是凡与六道众生一样，有悲哀的事情、痛苦的事情，一味的仰望诸佛拯救，我们世间人谁有痛苦的事情不可解，一念观世音菩萨就解脱了，这是实实在在的事情，就怕你不念，你一念，当时的危难就解除，众生悲哀，我也是一样悲哀，众生仰望<span class="GramE">著诸佛普</span>救、我也是仰望<span class="GramE">著诸佛普</span>救。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">世</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">尊。由我供养观音如来。<span class="GramE">蒙彼如来</span>。授我如幻。闻<span class="GramE">熏闻修</span>。金刚三昧。与佛如来。<span class="GramE">同慈力</span>故。令我身成三十二应。<span class="GramE">入诸国土</span>。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这一段文是总起来发明全体大用，「由我供养观音如来」，这是观世音菩萨供养观世音佛，「<span class="GramE">蒙彼如来</span>」，<span class="GramE">蒙彼观世音</span>如来，「授我如幻，闻<span class="GramE">熏闻修</span>，金刚三昧」，授给我如幻，世间上一切万事万物，无非是<span class="GramE">如幻如化</span>，转眼就成空，用这个意思「闻<span class="GramE">熏闻修</span>」，我起初用这个闻性，由这里开的悟，还是用这个闻性来熏、用闻性来修行，时时刻刻不离开这个闻性，以这个闻性为本位，才成了「金刚三昧」，这个金刚三昧就<span class="GramE">能破无明见佛性</span>，由这个金刚三昧，「与佛如来，<span class="GramE">同慈力</span>故」，我以这个如<span class="GramE">幻闻熏闻修</span>金刚三昧，「令我身成三十二应」，令我得成<span class="GramE">三十二应身</span>，现<span class="GramE">一切相度一切</span>众生，「<span class="GramE">入诸国土</span>」，不是光在一个<span class="GramE">娑</span>婆世界，其余的诸佛国土，我都<span class="GramE">去度化</span>众生。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="三十二應"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">三十二应<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="應現聖乘四"></a><span class="GramE"><span style="mso-bookmark: 應現聖乘四"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">应现圣乘</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="mso-bookmark: 應現聖乘四"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">四<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="一菩薩"></a><span class="GramE"><span style="mso-bookmark: 一菩薩"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">一</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="mso-bookmark: 一菩薩"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"> 菩萨<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">世</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">尊。<span class="GramE">若诸菩萨</span>入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>。进修无漏。<span class="GramE">胜解现圆</span>。<span class="GramE">我现佛身</span>。而为说法。令其解脱。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这一段文，这是观世音菩萨应化身，<span class="GramE">示现三十二应身</span>，「<span class="GramE">世</span>尊，<span class="GramE">若诸菩萨</span>入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>」，这里说菩萨入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>，<span class="GramE">这三摩地有</span>深有浅，大乘也有三<span class="GramE">摩地、小乘也</span>有三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>，这是大乘里头的三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>，这是<span class="GramE">示现四圣法</span>界，三十二应的头一应，<span class="GramE">若诸菩萨</span>他已经入了正定正受的地位，「进修无漏」，这个佛法到了究竟上，<span class="GramE">得修无漏行</span>，这个漏大端有<span class="GramE">三</span>：<span class="GramE">欲漏、色漏、</span>无色漏。有漏就是凡夫，<span class="GramE">欲漏是欲界天</span>，有六层：四天王天、<span class="GramE">忉</span>利天、夜摩天、<span class="GramE">兜率天</span>、化乐天、他化自在天，这六<span class="GramE">层欲界天</span>都有<span class="GramE">男婚女</span>配；<span class="GramE">色界十八</span>天：离生喜乐地、定生喜乐地、<span class="GramE">离喜妙乐</span>地、<span class="GramE">舍</span>念清净地，这十八层<span class="GramE">色界天</span>人用的功夫，都有阶级，离生喜乐地有三层、定生喜乐地有三层、<span class="GramE">离喜妙乐</span>地有三层、<span class="GramE">舍</span>念清净地有九层，一共<span class="GramE">十八层天</span>，这都在有漏<span class="GramE">里头，</span>还有形色<span class="GramE">没尽，欲漏是</span>有男女<span class="GramE">婚配没尽</span>；无色漏有四<span class="GramE">空天</span>：空无边处天、识无边处天、无所有处天、<span class="GramE">非想非非想处</span>天，这四<span class="GramE">层天漏在空里头，</span>空是无色漏，这个地方要醒悟这个道理，能把这三<span class="GramE">种漏都</span>脱离了，这才能到无漏的地位，这个地方在本位上说，「<span class="GramE">若诸菩萨</span>入三<span class="GramE">摩地</span>，进修无漏」的大法，<span class="GramE">漏尽一通</span>，这就要<span class="GramE">成佛了</span>，他进修无漏，不能说完全的无漏，也就快到了无漏的地步，还要加工进步的修，「<span class="GramE">胜解现圆</span>」，他这个<span class="GramE">优胜解悟的</span>这个理，发现圆融无碍了，没有缺欠的地方，就在这一点就圆满了，观世音菩萨说，「<span class="GramE">我现佛身</span>」，这位菩萨<span class="GramE">就是等觉的</span>菩萨了，与佛差不多了，<span class="GramE">与佛差一个</span>阶级了，<span class="GramE">等觉以上</span>就是妙<span class="GramE">觉果海的佛位</span>，<span class="GramE">观世音菩萨缺现前这一念还没</span>清净，「<span class="GramE">我现佛身</span>，而为说法」，<span class="GramE">漏尽通</span>了，这个地方才可以<span class="GramE">胜解现圆</span>，优胜的地方现出圆融无碍的境界，这是最末后的<span class="GramE">一著</span>，说这个究竟无漏的大法，该怎么样呢？「令其解脱」，他<span class="GramE">还有欲漏未</span>尽，没得解脱，若<span class="GramE">漏尽通</span>了，这就完全了，这是<span class="GramE">说等觉</span>的菩萨。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="二獨覺"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">二独觉<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸有</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">学。<span class="GramE">寂静妙明</span>。<span class="GramE">胜妙现圆</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现独觉身</span>。而为说法。令其解脱。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「<span class="GramE">若诸有</span>学」，<span class="GramE">这说有学位</span>，和无学位就差一步，有<span class="GramE">学虽有欲漏</span>未尽，「<span class="GramE">寂静妙明</span>」，到了寂然不动、静而无声，到了寂静的地方，怎么<span class="GramE">叫妙明</span>？心里明明白白的，入了寂静，他这个明还<span class="GramE">不能著</span>在寂静上，<span class="GramE">妙是不作</span>寂静的思想议论，不可思议<span class="GramE">才叫妙</span>、才叫明，就是一个明明白白的，这个地方引出「<span class="GramE">寂静妙明</span>」，大家想想，也<span class="GramE">不是口议</span>、也不是心思，这<span class="GramE">叫妙明</span>，在这个地方可以设身处地比量比量，怎么<span class="GramE">叫妙明</span>？虽然他没到无学位，在有学位上，到了<span class="GramE">寂静妙明</span>的境界，「<span class="GramE">胜妙现圆</span>」，他这个不思议的境界圆满了，「我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>」，我在他现前指点他，「<span class="GramE">现独觉身</span>」，<span class="GramE">独觉是</span>出于无佛<span class="GramE">世</span>，他自己独自觉悟的，<span class="GramE">独觉是</span>依著<span class="GramE">缘觉立</span>的名字，<span class="GramE">缘觉是</span>依十二因缘法悟道，<span class="GramE">听佛说</span>十二因缘，二者都是中乘圣人，有修<span class="GramE">独觉者</span>，我「<span class="GramE">现独觉身</span>，而为说法，令其解脱。」<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="三緣覺"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">三缘觉<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸有</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">学。断十二缘。<span class="GramE">缘断胜性</span>。<span class="GramE">胜妙现圆</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现缘觉身</span>。而为说法。令其解脱。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「<span class="GramE">若诸有</span>学」，这个有学不是平常的讲法，有学问，佛教讲有学是还有应当学的还没学，还有可学的，学到无学位，再没有可学的了，就成了，是这么<span class="GramE">个</span>讲法，「断十二缘」，断了这十二种因缘，这十二种因缘是人生死的一条大路，关乎三<span class="GramE">世</span>，前世有无明为因，到现世做无明的事又是因，做来世的结果，过去、现在、未来这是三<span class="GramE">世</span>，分十二<span class="GramE">个</span>因缘，头一个因缘是无明，无明就是不明白，就是糊涂！由「无<span class="GramE">明缘行</span>」，由无明就做糊涂事，「<span class="GramE">行缘识</span>」，行什么事就有什么认识，「<span class="GramE">识缘名色</span>」，名色是人投胎，有这么<span class="GramE">个</span>名字和形色，<span class="GramE">一做胎就</span>叫名色，「<span class="GramE">名色缘</span>六入」，<span class="GramE">一做胎就</span>有六入，<span class="GramE">不叫眼</span>、耳、鼻、舌、身、意，「六<span class="GramE">入缘触</span>」，六根触六尘，不加分别就叫触，「<span class="GramE">触缘受</span>」，一生下来就吃奶、穿衣，「<span class="GramE">受缘爱</span>」，他吃母亲<span class="GramE">的奶就爱</span>他母亲，「<span class="GramE">爱缘取</span>」，长大了不光爱他母亲，爱什么取什么，「<span class="GramE">取缘有</span>」，取什么有什么就著住了，「有缘生」，他今生有什么习惯来生就<span class="GramE">有受生</span>，「<span class="GramE">生缘老</span>死，<span class="GramE">忧悲苦恼</span>」，再生下来，又经过<span class="GramE">幼而壮、壮而</span>老、老而死，有生必有老死，该怎么办呢？最后是<span class="GramE">忧悲苦恼</span>，一共十二支，过去的二支，无明、行、识，现在的<span class="GramE">名色至有</span>七支，生、老死二支是未来的，这叫十二因缘，「<span class="GramE">若诸有</span>学，断十二缘」，想修行断这十二因缘，不顺生死转，就修还灭门，你把十二因缘断了，无明灭<span class="GramE">乃至生灭</span>、老死灭，<span class="GramE">一</span>灭<span class="GramE">一切灭</span>，这是十二因缘还灭门，顺则<span class="GramE">生凡、逆则生圣</span>，「<span class="GramE">缘断胜性，胜妙现圆</span>」，在这里胜妙境<span class="GramE">界现圆</span>了，「我于<span class="GramE">彼前，现缘觉身</span>，而为说法，令其解脱」，我就<span class="GramE">往彼面前现缘觉身</span>而为说法，令其得解脱。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="四聲聞"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">四声闻<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸有</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">学。得四<span class="GramE">谛</span>空。<span class="GramE">修道入灭</span>。<span class="GramE">胜性现圆</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现声闻身。而为说法。令其解脱。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这是观世音菩萨的愿力，「<span class="GramE">若诸有</span>学，得四<span class="GramE">谛</span>空」，设若有学者欲「得四<span class="GramE">谛</span>空」，还没成就，未能到无学位，先解四<span class="GramE">谛</span>，苦、集、灭、道叫四<span class="GramE">谛</span>；<span class="GramE">苦集是</span>世间的因果、<span class="GramE">灭道是</span>出世的因果，怎么<span class="GramE">个理呢</span>？人要知道<span class="GramE">知苦断集、慕灭</span>修道，我们人在世间上有诸般的痛苦，大端就有八苦，零星<span class="GramE">的苦那就</span>说不尽了，八<span class="GramE">苦是</span>什么呢？爱别离苦、<span class="GramE">怨憎会苦</span>、求不得苦、五阴炽盛苦、<span class="GramE">生苦、老苦</span>、病苦、<span class="GramE">死苦</span>，这八<span class="GramE">苦是</span>人人脱不了的。生下来就哭，老了六根不遂，病不是好受的事情，临死如<span class="GramE">活马去</span>皮，更不好受，谁也免不了；「爱别离苦」，恩爱的夫妻，死一个，这也是苦，「<span class="GramE">怨憎会苦</span>」，你越怨恨他、讨厌他，天天还要聚会，还得一块做事，这也是苦；「求不得苦」，想求的得不到也是苦；「五<span class="GramE">蕴炽盛苦</span>」，五<span class="GramE">蕴</span>是色、受、想、行、识，色<span class="GramE">蕴</span>是有形有色的身体，他不能独立，就得享受衣、食、住，这个享受是从那里来的？得想<span class="GramE">主意为衣</span>、食、住，你得实行实做，人家行你不能行，还得学知识，有<span class="GramE">这个色身就</span>连带著后边的四样，这叫「五<span class="GramE">蕴炽盛苦</span>」，<span class="GramE">炽</span>是拿火炽在身上，烧的难过，我们<span class="GramE">为了衣</span>、食、住，哪个人没有痛苦？大家想想，佛<span class="GramE">说的四谛</span>法，这苦<span class="GramE">谛</span>是从那里来的？自己招来的，<span class="GramE">知苦要断集</span>，知道是苦，不要再招集苦因，<span class="GramE">知苦断集</span>这个道理，<span class="GramE">怎么断呢</span>？<span class="GramE">就是慕灭修道</span>，你<span class="GramE">想灭苦</span>就得修道，你<span class="GramE">羡慕寂灭</span>，就要<span class="GramE">灭有归空，怎么灭法</span>？得修道，<span class="GramE">不</span>修道不能<span class="GramE">灭苦，你灭</span>了凡情<span class="GramE">，寂灭才</span>现出，「生灭<span class="GramE">灭</span>已<span class="GramE">，寂灭为</span>乐」，把<span class="GramE">生灭法灭</span>完了，才<span class="GramE">成寂灭</span>之道，<span class="GramE">先是销灭</span>、后<span class="GramE">是寂灭</span>，都是一个字，这<span class="GramE">一个灭字</span>做两样讲，修到「<span class="GramE">胜性现圆</span>」，胜了<span class="GramE">理欲交徵</span>，他心里得到这个理，他把心里所欲的这个苦胜过了，这<span class="GramE">是胜性</span>，<span class="GramE">依著慕道</span>的<span class="GramE">心把苦</span>因苦果都给他放下了，一定<span class="GramE">修寂灭</span>的功夫，<span class="GramE">修寂灭</span>的这就叫道，修道就把世间的妄想灭了，妄想<span class="GramE">是个根</span>，不<span class="GramE">把它灭了</span>，<span class="GramE">苦是</span>去不掉的，「胜性现圆」，胜理胜过私欲，世间的欲望不让生长起来，所以才能修道，他因有修道的思想，还没修到圆满，「我于彼前，现声闻身」，所以观世音菩萨于彼面前现声闻身，声闻是小乘圣人的一个名字，他还没离开佛说法的声，他没离开耳朵那个闻，他听佛说法，做有为法解，声闻是小乘的根性，不能直接入真空之理，「而为说法」，观世音菩萨现身为他说知苦、断集、慕灭、修道四真谛的道理，「令其解脱」，令其解脱苦恼。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="應現天身七"></a><span class="GramE"><span style="mso-bookmark: 應現天身七"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">应现天身</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="mso-bookmark: 應現天身七"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">七<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="一梵王身"></a><span class="GramE"><span style="mso-bookmark: 一梵王身"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">一</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="mso-bookmark: 一梵王身"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"> <span class="GramE">梵</span>王身<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。<span class="GramE">欲心明悟</span>。<span class="GramE">不犯欲尘</span>。欲身清净。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现<span class="GramE">梵</span>王身。而为说法。令其解脱。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这<span class="GramE">段文说的高等</span>的凡夫，「若诸众生」，设若众生，「<span class="GramE">欲心明悟</span>」，他<span class="GramE">这个心欲想</span>著明白醒悟，不明心见性，这是<span class="GramE">欲界凡</span>夫，他但<span class="GramE">求明悟，欲界想明白色界天</span>的理和<span class="GramE">无色界天的</span>理，「<span class="GramE">不犯欲尘</span>」，不犯六欲的尘，六欲是<span class="GramE">眼欲色、耳欲声、鼻欲香、舌欲味</span>、<span class="GramE">身上欲触</span>、<span class="GramE">心里头欲法</span>，这是<span class="GramE">说欲界</span>欲<span class="GramE">想到色界上去</span>，不犯<span class="GramE">六欲之尘</span>，这<span class="GramE">是欲爱的</span>心，「欲身清净」，欲想身清净的得生<span class="GramE">到色界上去</span>，这个清净不是佛法的清净AN&gt;不得了，「我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>，现梵王身，而为说法，令其解脱」，观世音菩萨说，我在他面前现梵王身而为说法，令其解脱，得一步一步的来，他这是有次序，他不懂佛法，菩萨就现梵王身，说梵王天的法，他这是离开欲界到色界的初一步，大家想想，这与成佛道相差多远，你直接给他说佛法他不信，就得为他说梵天的修行法，那是讲离生喜乐地、定生喜乐地、离喜妙乐地、舍念清净地。离生喜乐，他是离开<span class="GramE">欲界生</span>欢喜心，「离生喜乐地」没有定力，要学「定生喜乐地」，得著定，还有喜乐的心，有喜也不对，我离开这个欢喜，叫「<span class="GramE">离喜妙乐</span>地」，<span class="GramE">到了妙乐上</span>，<span class="GramE">离喜妙乐</span>，还有乐，<span class="GramE">有乐还不对</span>，「<span class="GramE">舍</span>念清净地」，<span class="GramE">把乐的</span>这个念头都<span class="GramE">舍</span>了，这才清净，这<span class="GramE">是色界十八</span>天的阶级，大家得要知道，<span class="GramE">觉著</span>这个实在不错了，所以菩萨现<span class="GramE">梵</span>王身，满他的愿，「而为说法，令其解脱」，<span class="GramE">解脱欲界之</span>苦，生<span class="GramE">到色界上去</span>，这是一段「离生喜乐地」三层，<span class="GramE">是初禅</span>，「定生喜乐地」三层，是二禅，「<span class="GramE">离喜妙乐</span>地」三层，是三禅，「<span class="GramE">舍</span>念清净地」九层，是四禅，一共<span class="GramE">十八层天</span>。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">二 帝<a name="二帝釋"></a>释<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。欲为天主。<span class="GramE">统领诸天</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现帝释身</span>。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「若诸众生」，设若有众生，「欲为天主，<span class="GramE">统领诸天</span>」，<span class="GramE">欲界天王</span>是<span class="GramE">帝释天</span>，常说三十三天在须弥山的中腰，南八天、北八天、东八天、西八天，<span class="GramE">帝释居中</span>，在须弥山顶，这叫三十三天，他欲<span class="GramE">统领著</span>三十三天，观世音菩萨就在他面前<span class="GramE">现帝释身</span>而为说法，令其成就他这个愿力。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="三自在天"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">三自在天<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。欲身自在。游行十方。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现<span class="GramE">自在天身</span>。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">自在天<span class="GramE">是欲界的</span>有顶天，在<span class="GramE">欲界天</span>的顶上叫自在天，「欲身自在，游行十方」，这是他的愿力，观世音菩萨就现身为他说法，令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="四大自在天"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">四大自在天<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。欲身自在。飞行虚空。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现大<span class="GramE">自在天身</span>。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「若诸众生，欲身自在，飞行虚空」，若有众生，欲身得自由自在，任运的飞行虚空，他以空中飞行这是成道了，其实这是凡夫，观世音菩萨现大<span class="GramE">自在天身</span>，为他说法，令他成就他的愿力，大自在天，<span class="GramE">是色界有</span>顶天，是<span class="GramE">色界十八层天</span>顶。<span lang="EN-US">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="五天將軍"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">五天将军<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">    <o:p>    &nbsp;   </o:p> </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細>&nbsp;</o:p>  </SPAN></SPAN></P>  <P class=MsoNormal style=" text-justify: inter-ideograph; text-align: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="六四天王"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">六四天王<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></span></b></span></p>
<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。<span class="GramE">爱统世界</span>。保护众生。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现四天王身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「若诸众生，<span class="GramE">爱统世界</span>」，若诸众生，爱统理世界，「保护众生」，保护世界上一切所有众生，「我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>，现四天王身，而为说法，令其成就」，四天王天在须弥山腰，这个天还在地<span class="GramE">居天，忉</span>利天就是<span class="GramE">帝释天</span>，在三十三天，位在须弥山顶，这二种天都叫<span class="GramE">地居天</span>，虽然是高，还没离开地皮，山还在地上，观世音菩萨现四天王身为其说法，成就其爱护世界、保卫众生的志愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="七天王太子"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">七天王太子<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。爱生天宫。驱使鬼神。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现四天王国太子身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">或为四天王，或为四天王的太子，爱驱使鬼神，都有五戒十善的因，就能感生四王天的果，菩萨为其说法，令他成就驱使鬼神的志愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="應現國民十二"></a><span class="GramE"><span style="mso-bookmark: 應現國民十二"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">应现国民</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="mso-bookmark: 應現國民十二"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">十二<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="一人王"></a><span class="GramE"><span style="mso-bookmark: 一人王"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">一</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="mso-bookmark: 一人王"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體"> 人王<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。乐为人王。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现人王身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这<span class="GramE">是说现国王</span>身为治国安邦的众生说法，成就其所愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="二長者"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">二长者<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US">        <o:p></o:p> </span></b></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。<span class="GramE">爱主族姓</span>。世间推让。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现长者身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span class="GramE"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">菩萨随类现身</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">，为<span class="GramE">族姓者</span>，现长者身，说世间善法引入佛道，令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="三居士"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">三居士<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。爱谈名言。清净自居。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现居士身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">现居士身为说三<span class="GramE">皈</span>、五戒、六度万行等法，令其成就佛道。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="四宰官"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">四宰官<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。爱治国土。剖断<span class="GramE">邦邑</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现宰官身</span>。而为说法。令其成就。</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p></o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">设有众生，爱治理国土，「剖断<span class="GramE">邦邑</span>」，就是<span class="GramE">分疆裂</span>土，<span class="GramE">邦</span>是国的边界、<span class="GramE">邑</span>是州县的边界，分析开了，「我于<span class="GramE">彼前，现宰官身</span>，而为说法，令其成就」，菩萨<span class="GramE">就现宰官身</span>，主持国家的大事，<span class="GramE">宰官按</span>世间法说，吏部天官为大主宰、户部地官是大主财，一共是六部，<span class="GramE">还有春官</span>、夏官、<span class="GramE">秋官、冬官</span>，春、夏、秋、冬四部，加上天官、地官，这是六部大臣，这<span class="GramE">得现宰官身</span>而为说法，成就其志愿，<span class="GramE">扶救众生</span>。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="五術士"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">五术士<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。<span class="GramE">爱诸数术</span>。<span class="GramE">摄卫自居</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现婆罗门身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">「若诸众生，<span class="GramE">爱诸数术，摄卫</span>自居」，设若有人爱好算数，<span class="GramE">驱神驱</span>鬼的法术，<span class="GramE">能摄受自</span>心卫护自己，「我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>，现婆罗门身，而为说法，令其成就」，<span class="GramE">菩萨就现婆罗门</span>身，而为说法。婆罗门在印度，<span class="GramE">佛没出世</span>前就有，佛出世都是出生在婆罗门家，他能守四戒，不杀、盗、<span class="GramE"> </span>、<span class="GramE">妄</span>，佛要降生，会选择清净的地方，将来弥勒佛出世也是出生在婆罗门家，那时叫龙华胜会，我们这时候正是末<span class="GramE">法垂秋</span>，正法一千年、像法一千年、末法没定数。佛法在世间有兴的时候、有没的时候，就是关乎人的机缘善根成熟没成熟，人的机缘成熟了，这佛法就要出现了，这个地方这意思略说几句，当时下婆罗门在印度<span class="GramE">很盛，佛入灭以后</span>，佛法在印度就慢慢的没有了，近代世界各国，有智慧的人，看见佛经他知道这种道理有根本，从根本上解决，旁的道门都说不到究竟，因此都要研究佛法。前几年印度有位领事官和我讨论过，问这<span class="GramE">涅盘</span>有多少种？我给<span class="GramE">他说了一些</span>，他说我们印度当下立了一个佛学研究会，他和我研究一次就走了，一见面就说他是婆罗门。<span class="GramE">释迦佛本是</span>婆罗门的种族降生，<span class="GramE">后来佛才说法</span>，建立佛教，<span class="GramE">佛入灭</span>后，婆罗门就不信TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"&gt;<span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有男子。好学出家。<span class="GramE">持诸戒律</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现比丘身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">         <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有男人喜欢离开家庭，<span class="GramE">行持佛教</span>里诸般的戒律，<span class="GramE">比丘戒有二百五十</span>条，受<span class="GramE">了戒才可以</span>持戒，比丘翻<span class="GramE">乞</span>士，在家学佛的人可以称居士，有清高出尘的志愿，就叫居士，出了家就叫比丘，引导不信佛法的教他求学，<span class="GramE">乞</span>士是上<span class="GramE">乞</span>佛法以资法身、下<span class="GramE">乞</span>斋饭以养生命，当下南洋群岛仍有比丘托 化斋，自己不能做饭吃，不要产业，到了中国风俗不同，就变化了，也可以自食其力，也有国家送产业的，也有自己置产业的，就不用上街托 了，制度就变了，观世音菩萨现比丘身而为说法，成就比丘的资格。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="七比丘尼"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">七比丘尼<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有女人。好学出家。<span class="GramE">持诸禁</span>戒。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。现比丘尼身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">设有女人，好学出家，<span class="GramE">远尘离垢，</span>比丘尼翻<span class="GramE">乞</span>士女，持比丘尼的戒条，多过比丘的戒条一倍，菩萨现身说法，成就她的志愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="八優婆塞"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">八优婆塞<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有男子。<span class="GramE">乐持五戒</span>。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现优婆塞身</span>。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">优<span class="GramE">婆塞翻近事男</span>，侍奉佛法的近人，菩萨现身为他说五戒十善法，令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="九優婆夷"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">九优婆夷<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有女子。五戒自居。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现优婆夷身</span>。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">优<span class="GramE">婆夷是</span>近侍女，侍奉佛法接近的女人，佛教之中有四众弟子，这是在家二众弟子，菩萨现身为其说法成就五戒十善。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="十內政女人"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">十内政女人<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有女人。内政立身。以修家国。我<span class="GramE">于彼前</span>。<span class="GramE">现女主身</span>。及      <st1:personname w:st="on" productid="國">      国     </st1:personname> 夫人。命妇大家。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这是说若有女子，欲在朝中执政，修身齐家，菩萨满一切众生愿，「现女主身」，也可以说是女皇帝及大臣夫人、命妇，知识高、受国家封，叫诰命夫人，大家，大家的家字在这里念姑，他这个字用是用大家，大家是什么意思呢？可以给国王诰命的夫人，可以做师父，就是女师，那时不同现在有学堂，就称大家，而为其说法，令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="十一童男"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">十一童男<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有众生。不坏男根。我于彼前。现童男身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">这是根本的童子，佛法里有童男身发心修行，童男身童女身修行容易成道，文殊菩萨恨本上就是童男身，观音菩萨也现童男身，令其成就道业。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="十二童女"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">十二童女<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有处女。爱乐处见。不求侵暴。我于彼前。现童女身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">处女是未曾出嫁的女人，观音菩萨现身说法，成就她的志愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="應現天龍等九"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">应现天龙等九<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="一天眾"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">一天众<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有诸天。乐出天伦。我现天身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">底下说成就他所厌离的，人间受苦的时候多，生厌烦心，愿意离开，按天上受乐的时候多，享天堂的福，他怎么还有厌离的心？在佛经上仔细考查，天上有五衰相现，也有生死之苦，就愿意脱离，观世音菩萨现身说法，令其脱离五衰现相之苦。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="二龍眾"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">二龙众<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有诸龙。乐出龙伦。我现龙身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">龙有两种，分天龙、海龙，有两种苦处，他总想脱他这一类，不愿在龙里头，他有两种苦难：一是金翅岛、一是热沙之苦，大鹏金翅鸟，常常吃龙，所以是苦，龙身有鳞，鳞里生虫，在热沙打滚，免除他的难过，所以是苦，观世音菩萨现龙身为其说法，满其所愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="三藥叉"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">三药叉<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若有药叉。乐度本伦。我于彼前。现药叉身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">药叉也有说是夜叉的，能飞行，他不愿做药叉，喜欢脱离他的本伦，观世音菩萨现身为他说法，也成就其所愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="四乾達婆"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">四乾达婆<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若乾达婆。乐脱其伦。我于彼前。现乾达婆身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">乾达婆翻寻香，那里有香味他就去，也翻乐神，他能歌舞，他想脱离本伦，观世音菩萨现身说法，也成就其所愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="五阿修羅"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">五阿修罗<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若阿修罗。乐脱其伦。我于彼前。现阿修罗身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">阿修罗翻无端正。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="六緊那羅"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">六紧那罗<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若紧那罗。乐脱其伦。我于彼前。现紧那罗身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">紧那罗也翻疑神，也翻歌神，这在天龙八部之中有这个名字，他要离开这一类，菩萨现身，也给他说说脱离的方法。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="七摩呼羅伽"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">七摩呼罗伽<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若摩呼罗伽。乐脱其伦。我于彼前。现摩呼罗伽身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">摩呼罗伽是一种大蟒，也叫大腹蟒神，他要脱离其伦，菩萨就现身给他说法，令他成就，脱离蟒身之苦。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="八常人眾"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">八常人众<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">      <o:p>      &nbsp;     </o:p> </span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸众生。乐人修人。我现人身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">有些众生，喜欢生于人道，菩萨给他说法，成就他的志愿。<span lang="EN-US">      <o:p></o:p> </span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><a name="九非人眾"><span style="COLOR: #333399; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">九非人众<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p> </span></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><span lang="EN-US" style="COLOR: black; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">     <o:p>     &nbsp;    </o:p> </span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-JUSTIFY: inter-ideograph; TEXT-ALIGN: justify"><span style="mso-bookmark: 六入"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><span style="COLOR: teal; FONT-FAMILY: 新細明體">若诸非人。有形无形。有想无想。乐度其伦。我于彼前。皆现其身。而为说法。令其成就。<span lang="EN-US">       <o:p></o:p>
